### All the decisions have a non WTT dependent and a WTT version.

economy_decisions = {
	SOV_replace_baku_with_volga_ural_basin = { #accelerate oil decisions if lost azerbaijan
		
		icon = oil

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 249
			} 
		}
		available = {
			249 = {
				OR = {
					has_resistance = no
					AND = {
						compliance > 30
						resistance < 75
					}
				}
			}
			has_tech = excavation2
			owns_state = 249
			has_full_control_of_state = 249
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 5			
			NOT = {
				has_idea = generic_resource_extraction_effort
				has_full_control_of_state = 229
			}			
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = {
				has_full_control_of_state = 229
				has_tech = excavation_a
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 100
		days_remove = 210

		modifier = {
		}

		complete_effect = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = generic_resource_extraction_effort
				days = 120
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		remove_effect = { 
			set_country_flag = prospect_volga_ural_basin
		}	
	}

	develop_petsamo_nickel_deposits = { #722 - transferred from Norwegian-Finnish decision - Fantom
		
		icon = chromium
		
		available = {
			722 = {
				OR = {
					has_resistance = no
					AND = {
						compliance > 30
						resistance < 75
					}
				}
			}
			has_tech = excavation1
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 722
				}				
				AND = {
					any_country = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						has_full_control_of_state = 722
					}
				}
			}
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 2

				has_idea = generic_resource_extraction_effort
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 722
			} 
		}
		
		visible = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 722
				}				
				AND = {
					any_country = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						has_full_control_of_state = 722
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				any_other_country = {
					has_decision = develop_petsamo_nickel_deposits
				}
			}			
			772 = {
				NOT = {
					has_state_flag = petsamo_nickel_developed
				}
			}
		}
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		cost = 25
		days_remove = 60
		
		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 3
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				num_of_military_factories > 9
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 9
			}
		}
		remove_effect = { 
			722 = { set_state_flag = petsamo_nickel_developed }
			722 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = chromium	### Represents nickel
					amount = 8
				}
				add_resource = {
					type = tungsten	### Represents nickel
					amount = 4
				}
			}
		}
	}

	expand_cuban_chromium = { # 
		
		icon = chromium

		allowed = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
    				has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				}
			}			
		}

		available = {
			315 = {
				OR = {
					has_resistance = no
					AND = {
						compliance > 30
						resistance < 75
					}
				}
			}
			owns_state = 315
			has_full_control_of_state = 315
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 6
			has_tech = excavation4
			NOT = {
				has_idea = generic_resource_extraction_effort
			}			
		}
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 315
			} 
		}

		visible = {
			owns_state = 315
			has_full_control_of_state = 315
			315 = {
				NOT = {
					has_state_flag = { 
						flag = cuban_chromium_expanded 
						value = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 25
		days_remove = 60

		complete_effect = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = generic_resource_extraction_effort
				days = 30
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1
				chromium < 5
			}			
			modifier = {
				add = 4
				chromium < 1
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				date > 1942.01.01
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				num_of_military_factories > 50
			}			
		}
		remove_effect = { 
			add_to_variable = { var = cuban_chromium_duration value = 30 }
			315 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_state_flag = cuban_chromium_expanded
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = {
						flag = cuban_chromium_expanded
						value = 1
					}
				}
				else = {
					modify_state_flag = {
						flag = cuban_chromium_expanded
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}		
			315 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = chromium
					amount = 10
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = cuban_chromium_duration value = 30 compare = less_than }
				}
				set_variable = { var = cuban_chromium_duration value = 30 }
			}
		}		
	}

	exploit_marcona_iron = { # 492 -1943
		
		icon = steel

		allowed = {		
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
    				has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				}
			}		
		}

		available = {
			492 = {
				OR = {
					has_resistance = no
					AND = {
						compliance > 30
						resistance < 75
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 492
				}
				any_country = {
					is_puppet_of = ROOT
					has_full_control_of_state = 492
				}				
			}
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 4
			OR = {
				has_tech = excavation5
				AND = {
					has_tech = excavation3
					has_completed_focus = PRU_national_mining_administration
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_idea = generic_resource_extraction_effort
			}				
					
		}
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 492
			} 
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 492
				}
				any_country = {
					is_puppet_of = ROOT
					has_full_control_of_state = 492
				}				
			}
			NOT = {
				any_other_country = {
					has_decision = exploit_marcona_iron
				}
			}
			492 = {
				NOT = {
					has_state_flag = { 
						flag = marcona_iron_exploited 
						value = 2
					}
				}				
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 25
		days_remove = 60

		complete_effect = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = generic_resource_extraction_effort
				days = 30
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1
				steel < 5
			}			
			modifier = {
				add = 4
				steel < 1
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				date > 1942.01.01
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				num_of_military_factories > 50
			}			
		}
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = marcona_iron_duration value = 30 compare = less_than }
				}
				set_variable = { var = marcona_iron_duration value = 30 }
			}
		}		
		remove_effect = { 
			add_to_variable = { var = marcona_iron_duration value = 30 }
			492 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_state_flag = marcona_iron_exploited
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = {
						flag = marcona_iron_exploited
						value = 1
					}
				}
				else = {
					modify_state_flag = {
						flag = marcona_iron_exploited
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}				
			492 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = steel
					amount = 8
				}
			}
		}
	}

				}				
			}
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 4
			OR = {
				has_tech = excavation5
				AND = {
					has_tech = excavation3
					has_completed_focus = PRU_national_mining_administration
				}
			}	
					
		}
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 492
			}

			OR = {
				has_full_control_of_state = 492
				any_country = {
					is_puppet_of = ROOT
					has_full_control_of_state = 492
				}				
			}
			NOT = {
				any_other_country = {
					has_decision = exploit_marcona_iron_wtt
				}
			}			
			492 = {
				NOT = {
					has_state_flag = { 
						flag = marcona_iron_exploited 
						value = 2
					}
				}				
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 25
		days_remove = 60

		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 5
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0			
		}
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = marcona_iron_duration value = 30 compare = less_than }
				}
				set_variable = { var = marcona_iron_duration value = 30 }
			}
		}		
		remove_effect = { 
			add_to_variable = { var = marcona_iron_duration value = 30 }
			492 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_state_flag = marcona_iron_exploited
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = {
						flag = marcona_iron_exploited
						value = 1
					}
				}
				else = {
					modify_state_flag = {
						flag = marcona_iron_exploited
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}				
			492 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = steel
					amount = 8
				}
			}
		}	
	}
